<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</b></div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">On May 15, 2023, ParkerVision, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release which reported financial and operating results for the three months ended March 31, 2023. A copy of the press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">The information contained in this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1 hereto, has been &#8220;furnished&#8221; and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to liability under that section. The information in this Current Report shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing or document.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<body style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; padding: 0in 0.1in; cursor: auto;">
<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: right; font-size: 11pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt;"><b>&nbsp;Exhibit 99.1</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 14pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: center; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>ParkerVision Reports Profitable First Quarter <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="7" id="led384391F20232231679594586844">2023</a> </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>JACKSONVILLE</b><b>, Fla.,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="21x1" data-tblname="384392" data-tblv="7" id="led384392F20232231679594614065">May 15, 2023</a> </b>&#8211;<b> </b>ParkerVision, Inc. (OTCQB: PRKR) (&#8220;ParkerVision&#8221; or the "Company"), a developer and marketer of technologies and products for wireless applications, today announced results for the <a data-tblloc="13x1" data-tblname="384392" data-tblv="7" id="led384392F20232231679594637533">three months ended March 31, 2023</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>First Quarter <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="7" id="led384391F20232231679594669899">2023</a>&nbsp;Summary and Recent Developments</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company recognized $25 million in revenue from patent license and settlement agreements and, after recognizing contingent legal fees and expenses, reported net income of $13.1 million in the first quarter of 2023.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; margin: 0pt;">To date, the Company has resolved patent infringement actions filed in the Western District of Texas against Buffalo, Zyxel, Hisense and, most recently, Intel.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; margin: 0pt;">On May 4, 2023, the Company entered into a letter agreement with its litigation funder, receiving $5 million in new funding under its contingent payment agreement.&nbsp; The new funds will be used for working capital purposes.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company continues to await its hearing date in the appeal of the Qualcomm case from the Middle District of Florida.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Jeffrey Parker, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, commented, &#8220;Our profitable financial results this quarter indicate the significant impact of receiving licensing compensation for the unauthorized use of our technologies by others. We plan to continue to aggressively pursue licenses for our innovations both in and out of court.&nbsp; The patents that are the subject of our enforcement actions represent innovations that we have invested hundreds of millions of dollars in over the last fifteen years to develop and bring these technologies to market and which we believe have become a mainstay for infringing companies.</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Parker continued, "We expect to file additional enforcement actions in the near future as we continue to identify additional unauthorized users of our intellectual property.&nbsp;&nbsp; We anticipate that the $5 million in new funding allows us to continue to pursue enforcement of our patent rights without the need to raise additional equity capital for the foreseeable future."</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:center;margin:0pt;">&#65279;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>Financial Results</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision reported net income for the first quarter of <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="7" id="led384391F20232231679594889334">2023</a> of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F20232231679595832924">$13.1</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023441683203006676">$0.16</a> per common share, compared to a net income of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x2" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F20232231679595853429">$0.3</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x2" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F20232231679595868331">$0.00</a> per common share for the first quarter of <a data-tblloc="32x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="7" id="led384391F20232231679594923115">2022</a>.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 81pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">o</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The increase in net income is the result of $25 million in revenue recognized on a patent license and settlement agreement reached in February 2023, offset by contingent legal fees and expenses incurred related to the agreement.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

		</tr>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>About ParkerVision</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision, Inc. invents, develops and licenses cutting-edge, proprietary radio-frequency (RF) technologies that enable wireless solution providers to make and sell advanced wireless communication products. &nbsp;ParkerVision is engaged in a number of patent enforcement actions in the U.S. to protect patented rights that it believes are broadly infringed by others. For more information, please visit www.parkervision.com.<i> (PRKR-I)</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>
